No. Not just Numiz. Several projects, but Numiz is first to send out the press release.

Mitja, like I and several others are founders and investors in Numiz. KWF and KWPC are projects where Mitja and others are founders.

No. KWF is one of the funds that bring Numiz initial liquidity and will trade both the art token (FWA) and the Numiz token (there will be a token sale) on FLEX. KWPC is the podcast that will host investors, art dealers, art critics, artists (creators ‚Äî art, music, film) to run discussions and vote for which Numiz are best, and then hold auctions live on the podcast. For other projects it will be the same idea. But this is only one branch of what Numiz is doing. There are other things coming as well. This KWA fund is specifically for known and popular artists. Obviously the Numiz token will be listed on other exchanges as well. Most likely the Numiz token will be NZT, but we haven't finalized that decision yet. It was originally supposed to be CNZ when we still called the project CryptoNumiz, but we removed the word "crypto" from it, because we feel nowadays the word is redundant since pretty much everyone knows what crypto is, so we dropped that part and are calling it just Numiz; therefore, the ticker and token name has to change too.

Hope that answers your question
